<pictures>None< /pictures>< Text>
Best shop I've been to. Hands down. Been an avid reader of comics for a few years now, and I love my weekly trips to Ryan's.

The organization (both layout and product arrangment) and cleanliness cannot be matched. The wide range of collectibles, books and games are the widest I've seen in all my comics shop travels. Pricing is pretty spot on.

Be it Marvel or DC, they'll likely have all the newest stuff. Secondly, I've never been to a shop that supports independents so well. Great selection there.

My one knock: they have such a large set of regular readers that nabbing a new hot book can sometimes be difficult. However, they offer a subscription service to avoid that disappointment.

DO RECOMMEND.<//Text>

<text>Ryan's Comics is easily the best comic store, if not the best store in general I have ever been to. The staff are super friendly and helpful, and they're just nice people to hang out with. Ryan's has an open reading policy (You can read any of there books while you're there) which is awesome, and they have several TVs playing either cartoons, sports or Superhero movies and/or music playing so there is never weird awkward silence 0_o

I personally play Magic: The Gathering at Ryan's(they also do Yu-Gi-Oh! events), and the group of people there are really nice and helpful, they aren't super competitive like some other places. Everyone is just there to play and have a good time doing so. Also the tournaments at Ryan's are a lot of fun, really well organized and have outstanding prize support.

All in all, Ryan's Comics is a great store whether you like comics, card games, board games, or just want to hang out with some good, friendly people.<//text>< Response>

< Text>
Backstory - I was told I can haggle and be nicely priced if I bought a large bundle of cards. The store owner had then left 30 minutes before the store closed, leaving me with another employee who did not provide that service (though he felt the need to lie that she did do so during our call).

The 'owner' of the store screams unprofessional in his body language and how he carries himself over a phone call. Long story short, I had called to note my disastisfaction with the pricing on cards, noting to him they were 'severely' overpriced and if he had a return policy. But one of the first things that come out his mouth was how 'offended' he was at my language, my use of the word 'severely' because apparently it's productive to argue that his opinion/feelings over a price invalidates the customer's (when you do quick math, he was charging 80-90% markup for cards many cards) Most of our back and forth was him deflecting with emotional sensitivity and personal remarks. It was completely unproductive. It felt as though he could not hold a conversation with an unsastisfied customer without throwing in fallacies. 'I have NEVER dealt with this with all my customers'-- and I made it clear that logic doesn't work in reality. He confirmed he was willing to do trade-ins but couldn't offer a return (which I was fine with), but then decided to retain the tension with, 'but I'm going with my terms'. Again, I echoed that my sources were from a website (tcgplayer) plus other visits and that we can find a middle ground from there, but that wasn't before he kept challenging the pricing and the loctions I've been as if his were cheaper. Anyway, the conversation ended with him chuckling that 'it's just $15' to me stating 'then why are you being difficult' to him claiming 'Sir, you are triggered. I am going to hang up right now'. The irony. It felt like having a conversation with an emotional teenager who needed to reach for remarks to stay in their safe space. Fact is, there are no other prominent stores in the nearby area, but there are much better tcg services elsewhere, namely in the LA area. I hope Ryan can learn to hold conversations with people outside of this culture as this immaturity was something else. Looks can be deceiving.

I'm not here to pretend it wasn't my fault for not double-checking prices. But the lengths and reaches this store owner went, as if I was his buddy arguing politics, can only explain why cards are dirt cheap online. These rag-tag shops can't interact with non-socially awkward customers on the basic level of even a retail store.< /Text>

< Review>
Ok ladies, gentlemen and those whom think that eyebrows are the most important feature on your face... LISTEN UP!!!

For many years I had been waxing my eyebrows. Until I discovered threading. As many of you know, it's important to find someone whom knows that the moment you sit in their chair they know exactly what to do.

3 years ago I stumbled upon a salon that offered threading (Aaliyah's Beauty and Brows -Hillcrest Location). As I opened the door to the salon I was immediately mesmerized and greeted by Ayesha the owner. She asked me what services I was looking for and asked me to sit in her chair. 10-15 minutes later I sat up and I was given a mirror to see the end result. WOW WOW AND WOW, I loved everything about my eyebrows. They looked clean and sharp!!!

Fast forward to a couple years and found a new job in a different part of SD. Needless to say I traveled from where I now lived to Hillcrest and waited whatever time it was necessary for my girls (eyebrows) to receive the TLC that they are accustomed to.

In conversation Ayesha told me she was opening a salon in the Eastlake area (much closer to home). I was excited to here that many other humans were going to be able to experience what Aaliyah's Beauty and Brows is all about.

In one of my recent visits to her salon, we were discussing the option of Micro blading. It truly was a no brainer decision to have her do them. Appointment was booked bright and early. I arrived at the salon with much excitement, knowing that I was going to wake up everyday and have a beautiful set of eyebrows already on.

Ayesha is very meticulous, she told me exactly what to anticipate. We choose the color that best suited my skin tone. Measurements and preciseness started to occur. Throughout the entire process Ayesha would constantly ensure that I felt no pain. Almost 1 hr and 45 minutes  later, I was once again was given a mirror to look at the end result.

Needless to say I was in LOVE, I loved everything about my newly improved girls. The color, the preciseness of every "hair" was truly and utterly fabulous. Hands down and without a doubt in my heart, if you are interested in getting your eyebrows threaded or Micro Bladed, Aaliyah's Beauty and Brows is the place to go.

I decided to do this review because someone as devoted and as passionate as she is, should be recognized. I highly recommend her, she is the best at what she does!!! #browguru, #nobodytocuhesmybrowsbutayesha<//Review>

<Text>Probably my favorite Persian restaurant of the numerous Persian restaurants I have tried in California, east coast, and europe...yes seriously they have the best quality meat and best tasting meats! Hands down the best juiciest tender koubideh, shishlik(individual lollipops of rack of lamb nicely charred), gormeh sabzi, fesenjoon, tahdig that is so nice and crisp but doesnt break your teeth when you bite into it, and their special baghali gatogh which are BABY lima beans with a ton of dill and garlic(ask for some lemon wedges to really bring out the flavor), plus when they aren't busy they toast their baklava so the outside is crisp and the inside is juicy hot! Mmmmmm mmmm. Definitely go on a Monday or Tuesday so you have their full attention. Only thing that is lacking is the appetizers and salads compared to the fancier Persian restaurants which instead offer sabzi for free with a variety of herbs instead of just basil. Plus the fancier places would offer jeweled rices. Come here for the best meats and baby lima beans which I have not found anywhere</Text><response>None</response></record>

< Review>
This is the second time I have eaten here. Both times it's been outstanding!
My friend asked me to purchase a Groupon and so we went for an early Dinner.

It was spectacular.

Clean establishment, super friendly service and very helpful / informative on deciding what to choose and why without being pushy.
The Baklava is so fresh it just melts in your mouth.
My friend and I are very picky so for us to give a 5 Star rating says a lot.

This second time my Husband and I went for a late Lunch and again just loved everything.
From the warm welcome, cleanliness, to the beautifully prepared food.
Our appetizer the Roasted Eggplant  was so decadent.

We tried the cold and hot Tea and each loved our version of it.
If you go please, take advantage of the knowledgeable host. We thoroughly enjoyed learning details about the carefully hand blended Tea.

Between the Lunch Combo Kabob and my Joojeh Kabob we were in heaven.
The rice was moist / fluffy, and the meat tender / juicy.

I highly recommend  Didar to anyone.<//Review>

<text>Freshie Tea has severely decreased in quality over the past few months.

I would strongly not recommend ordering drinks from their Wix website as they don't check these orders so it would be easier for everyone to order in person or through another app. I placed an order an hour ahead of time with the drinks I wanted and that I would be picking up an hour later, when I arrived, none of the workers there even knew my order existed. They recreated my order there, making me a solid 20 minutes behind schedule. They did not speed up my order either, even though I clearly made the order an hour before anyone else in the store. The menu has changed since a few months ago, and they never updated their website, so one of the drinks that I ordered online wasn't even available. When I arrived to get my drinks, they recreated my order and wanted to charge me extra for the drink that had toppings included at a set price. Also, the website offered a 10% discount for doing pickup, and when they recreated my order there, I was charged full price. This is unacceptable, do not order online.

Also, the quality of the cups have decreased too. The cups used to be the cute looking plastic cups with caps that you see when you google Freshie Tea, but now they use flimsy and sad looking cups without the cute caps. It is up to each store on how they want to sell and package their stuff, but as a customer this is really disappointing, and deters me from coming back as the prices are expensive and the tea tastes similar to all boba stores,  nothing makes them stand out.

However, there is one thing that saves this store, and it is their worker's and their service. Albeit they could have done better regarding my order and possibly helping streamline it, but the attitudes of the workers here were decent. They weren't rude which was why the store got 3 stars instead of 1. I don't believe I will be going back for a while, but if I do, I will update this review if they improve their service and quality.

TLDR: Freshie Tea quality has decreased immensely over the past few months, the menu has changed, the cups have gotten worse, and most importantly of all, do not order off their website.</text>< Resp>

< Review>
Outstanding establishment!  If you are a connoisseur of traditional burger/sandwich shops this should be high on your priority list.  Great sandwich and fries.

If you are going for lunch, I suggest going early.  I got there right at 12 and found parking spot in lot on west side of the shop.  About 3-4 people ahead of me in line.  When I left at 12:30 there was no parking and 10-12 people waiting to order.  The small dinning area was full and tables outside were also filled.</Review>
